**Lipsa Mishra:** Give me a second.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 给我一秒钟。

**Marina Stojanovic:** This full screen. Perfect. Thank you so much.

**Marina Stojanovic:** 这个全屏。完美。非常感谢。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Okay. Um…. We have different processes when we are
doing the software development lifecycle. We have planning, we have
building, we have testing, then we have release, and we have operations.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
好的。我们在进行软件开发生命周期时有不同的流程。我们有规划、构建、测试，然后是发布和运营。

**Lipsa Mishra:** We are trying to showcase how we can use the Kapada
UI… AI to build different kind of.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 我们正试图展示如何使用Copado UI……AI来构建不同种类的。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Agents and automate all of them. Kapado AI platform
uses. 5 agents plan, build, test, release, and operate. How can it help
its accelerate development?

**Lipsa Mishra:** 智能体并自动化所有这些。Copado
AI平台使用5个智能体：计划、构建、测试、发布和运营。它如何能帮助加速开发？

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then score quality, reduced technical dApp, and
then we can have increased team productivity.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后评估质量，减少技术债务（technical
debt：指开发过程中为求快速而采取的非最优解决方案，未来需要额外工作来修复），然后我们可以提高团队生产力。

**Lipsa Mishra:** I'm going to showcase a little bit about how our
automation works right now. So, we have business analysts who take care
of our requirement phase.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
我将展示一下我们目前的自动化工作原理。我们有业务分析师负责我们的需求阶段。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Then they create the stories in JIRA, then we have
engineers.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后他们在JIRA中创建用户故事，然后我们有工程师。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Who write the code, refactor, do the unit testing, and
then we deploy them into production. So all of this can be done and
automated using the Capado pipelines.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
他们编写代码、重构、进行单元测试，然后我们将其部署到生产环境。所有这些都可以使用Copado管道来完成和自动化。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Let me showcase to you, um, special thanks to my
teammates Damien and, uh, Rob, who have done this, uh, you know, demo.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
让我向你展示一下，特别感谢我的队友Damien和Rob，他们做了这个演示。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Um, let me know when you're able to see my screen
here.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 当你能看到我的屏幕时，请告诉我。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Yep, we can see it now.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 是的，我们现在能看到了。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Using Kopado AI to extract requirements. From multiple
meeting transcripts.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 使用Copado AI从多个会议记录中提取需求。

**Lipsa Mishra:** First of all, when someone in a new chat, I will
upload.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 首先，当有人在一个新聊天中时，我会上传。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Transcript files.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 转录文件。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And once they're all loaded. We'll include this
prompt. Assume you are a top-performing senior.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
一旦它们全部加载完毕。我们将包含这个提示。假设你是一位顶尖的高级。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Salesforce Business Analyst, please analyze the
meeting transcripts and extract identified and perceived.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
Salesforce业务分析师，请分析会议记录并提取已识别和感知到的。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Business requirements for lead management, and use the
Moscow methodology to provide a clear sentence.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
潜在客户管理的业务需求，并使用MoSCoW方法（一种优先级排序技术，将需求分为Must-have,
Should-have, Could-have, Won't-have）提供一个清晰的句子。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Then, produce a matrix showing traceability between
business requirements. Pain points, use cases, use case scenarios.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
然后，生成一个矩阵，显示业务需求、痛点、用例、用例场景之间的可追溯性。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Personas or roles. Invest formatted user stories in
well-defined acceptance criteria.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
用户画像或角色。将格式化的用户故事投入到定义明确的验收标准中。

**Lipsa Mishra:** In the given, when, then. Format.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
在给定的“Given-When-Then”（一种用于编写验收测试的格式）格式中。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And as you can see…. The first provides requirements
using the Masco prioritization.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 正如你所看到的……第一个使用MoSCoW优先级排序法提供需求。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then the traceability matrix. Our business
requirement, the pain point, the use case.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后是可追溯性矩阵。我们的业务需求、痛点、用例。

**Lipsa Mishra:** The use case scenario, persona or role. The user story
and acceptance criteria for each.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 用例场景、用户画像或角色。每个的用户故事和验收标准。

**Lipsa Mishra:** As you can see, the business requirement in the
traceability matrix.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 正如你所看到的，可追溯性矩阵中的业务需求。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Is a summarized version of the actual requirement, so
lead scoring, model implementation.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 是实际需求的摘要版本，所以潜在客户评分、模型实施。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Must implement a lead scoring model that accurately
reflects lead quality and potential value.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
必须实施一个能够准确反映潜在客户质量和潜在价值的潜在客户评分模型。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Thank you so much. I'm going to showcase, like. Uh,
from a business analyst perspective.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 非常感谢。我将从业务分析师的角度来展示。

**Lipsa Mishra:** You saw how Demon was able to record multiple
workshops, push all of them to the Capado AI, and generate all of his
use case, which is going to populate in Jira.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
你看到了Demon如何能够记录多个研讨会，将它们全部推送到Copado
AI，并生成他所有的用例，这些用例将填充到Jira中。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Now, it goes to our, you know, engineer, who's going
to create that into a pack storage.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
现在，它交给了我们的工程师，他将把它创建到一个包存储中。

**Lipsa Mishra:** To actual code. Alright, I'll be demoing, uh, Kapado
AI platform, uh, from, uh.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 转化为实际代码。好的，我将从……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Like, Salesforce kind of implementation perspective.
Um, so I have the chat already generated, because it takes quite a bit
of time to go through this, uh, but I'll just walk through the features
that are kind of highlighted here.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
比如，Salesforce的实施视角。我已经生成了聊天记录，因为要过一遍这个需要相当长的时间，但我会简单介绍一下这里突出显示的特性。

**Lipsa Mishra:** So, basically, I gave, uh, our agent a prompt to
create a user story for us and gave it.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
所以，基本上，我给了我们的智能体一个提示，让它为我们创建一个用户故事，并给了它。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Um, some of the acceptance criteria here. So it's
regarding a case that's, uh, added and reopening the case status to in
progress when a comment is added.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
这里的一些验收标准。所以这是关于一个案例，当添加评论时，案例状态会重新打开为“进行中”。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And, uh, if the case has been closed for more than 10
days, then the user cannot add a comment.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
而且，如果案例已经关闭超过10天，那么用户就不能添加评论。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, so then it wrote out the user story in the format
that I asked it, giving some acceptance criteria.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
所以它按照我要求的格式写出了用户故事，并给出了一些验收标准。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And provided some technical considerations. Then I
switched over to the build agent, which is the agent that can actually.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
并提供了一些技术考虑。然后我切换到构建智能体，这是一个可以实际。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Code, and uh… I told it to create a trigger. On the
case comment object that satisfies the requirements of the story.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
编码的智能体，我告诉它在满足故事需求的案例评论对象上创建一个触发器。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And gave it some hints on things that I don't want to
see, like debug statements. There should be some error handling, things
like that.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
并给它一些我不希望看到的提示，比如调试语句。应该有一些错误处理，诸如此类。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, and then it…. Thought quite a bit, and then it
came up with this, um….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后它……想了很久，然后想出了这个……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Trigger handler class, was it, which…. Implements our
trigger hand, like, framework, which I asked it to use.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
触发器处理程序类，是吗，它……实现了我们的触发器处理框架，我让它使用的那个。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, and it is connected to our Salesforce. Sandbox
instance to pull metadata and read it, and then we'll spit out things
that.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
它连接到我们的Salesforce沙盒实例，以提取和读取元数据，然后我们会输出一些东西。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Are essentially connected to it. So that's what it did
here.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 基本上是与之相连的。所以这就是它在这里做的。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then, uh, it implemented the appropriate methods
based on, like, a comment being inserted or updated.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后，它根据评论的插入或更新等情况，实现了相应的方法。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Things like that. And then it had, um, some logic here
to, um….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 诸如此类。然后它有一些逻辑来……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, where is it? Over here. That will update the
status to reopen when the, uh, comment is added.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
它在哪里？在这里。当评论被添加时，它将更新状态为“重新打开”。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, then in the area added the error… sorry, the
exception handling here.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后在这个区域添加了错误……抱歉，是异常处理。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Put some debug statement, but obviously it tells us
that we can change this to whatever.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
放了一些调试语句，但显然它告诉我们可以把它改成任何我们想要的。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Framework we want. Um, and then it….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 我们想要的框架。然后它……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Made some additional changes. Uh, without me prompting
it.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 做了一些额外的改动。在我没有提示的情况下。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then it implemented, uh, the trigger…. Over here,
so that's the trigger that says….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后它实现了……触发器……在这里，所以那个触发器说……

**Lipsa Mishra:** You know, before insert, after insert, whatever. Run
the handler class, or run the logic that it previously wrote.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
你知道，在插入之前，插入之后，等等。运行处理程序类，或者运行它之前编写的逻辑。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Um… and add some comments here, and then, uh, I asked
it to write a test class, which is essentially a unit test for the code
that it generated.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
在这里添加一些注释，然后，我让它编写一个测试类，这基本上是它生成的代码的单元测试。

**Lipsa Mishra:** I told her that it should run as a portal user, so
essentially run as a customer to make sure that all the security stuff
works.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
我告诉它应该以门户用户的身份运行，所以基本上是以客户的身份运行，以确保所有的安全措施都有效。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And it should assert that things happen the way that
they should.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 并且它应该断言事情按照它们应该的方式发生。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, so then that's what it did, so…. And created this
test class. It has this setup method where it inserts test data, creates
the portal user.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
所以它就是这么做的……并创建了这个测试类。它有一个设置方法，可以插入测试数据，创建门户用户。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then it has the unit test, uh, for each, you know,
different scenario.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后它有针对每个不同场景的单元测试。

**Lipsa Mishra:** It has the asserts as well to make sure that the data
is.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 它也有断言，以确保数据是。

**Lipsa Mishra:** As it should after the test has run. Um, and then….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 测试运行后应该的样子。然后……

**Lipsa Mishra:** And it made some updates. To the trigger handler
class.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 它做了一些更新。对触发器处理程序类。

**Lipsa Mishra:** For some reason. Uh, but anyways…. Uh, then after
that, I switched to the test agent.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 出于某种原因。但总之……在那之后，我切换到了测试智能体。

**Lipsa Mishra:** To, um….

**Lipsa Mishra:** 为了……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Ask it to create some testing scenarios for manual
testing.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 让它为手动测试创建一些测试场景。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Um, and I told it to include detailed test steps,
including the object and field references in Salesforce.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
我告诉它要包含详细的测试步骤，包括Salesforce中的对象和字段引用。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Um, including any buttons or the pages that the user
needs to go to, so that it's very specific to Salesforce.

**Lipsa Mishra:**
包括用户需要去的任何按钮或页面，这样它就非常特定于Salesforce。

**Lipsa Mishra:** And then it generated the positive and negative test
cases, um, based on this user story.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 然后它根据这个用户故事生成了正面和负面的测试用例。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Uh, you know, talks about, you know, logging into

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:** Yeah, so generated that. And then I have another chat

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:** Demonstrate another one, which is the release agent,

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:** 所以……

**Lipsa Mishra:** Sorry, come on.

**Lipsa Mishra:** 抱歉，来吧。

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:** Stories that are deployed, so I asked it for a

**Lipsa Mishra:** 部署的故事，所以我向它请求一个发布。

**Lipsa Mishra:** This release name, what was released. And then it's,

**Lipsa Mishra:** 这个发布名称，发布了什么。然后它，你知道的。

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:** To test what we have coded is our, you know, scenarios
all included with positive scenarios, negative scenarios, any kind of

**Lipsa Mishra:**
来测试我们编码的内容，包括所有正面场景、负面场景、任何边缘情况场景，确保我们的质量非常好。然后我们使用我们的部署智能体来确保它上线。我们有发布智能体。

**Lipsa Mishra:** Which kinds of creative or release notes. So what I

**Lipsa Mishra:**

**Lipsa Mishra:**
我们不必第一天就说，让我们成为AI，SLDSC（软件开发生命周期），没有流程。我们可以从小步开始，比如，我们现在最大的痛点是什么？是编写代码文档吗？是创建用户故事吗？

**Lipsa Mishra:** Is it creation of your release notes? Maybe start with

**Lipsa Mishra:**
是创建你的发布说明吗？也许从那开始，然后我们只是想看看我们如何能使用所有这些不同的智能体。

**Lipsa Mishra:** To make our life more efficient, and make sure that we

**Lipsa Mishra:**

### 用例10：Raka Dhar & Julia Groza - AI驱动的元数据生成器

**Raka Dhar:** So, uh, Julia, if you could start up.

**Raka Dhar:** 那么，Julia，如果你能开始的话。

**Raka Dhar:** Hi, everyone! Good afternoon. I am Raka. And along with
Julia from engineering, uh, Ben and Tom Zorg, we're excited to walk you
through.

**Raka Dhar:** 大家好！下午好。我是Raka。我和工程部的Julia，以及Ben和Tom
Zorg，很高兴能带大家了解。

**Raka Dhar:** A tool which we have built. And named by ourselves an
AI-powered metadata generator.

**Raka Dhar:** 我们构建的一个工具，我们自己命名为AI驱动的元数据生成器。

**Raka Dhar:** Now, it sounds scary, but let me simplify it a bit.

**Raka Dhar:** 现在，这听起来可能有点吓人，但让我稍微简化一下。

**Raka Dhar:** Metadata is how. Your AI knows it's reading patient
records.

**Raka Dhar:** 元数据是你的AI知道它正在阅读病人记录的方式。

**Raka Dhar:** And not pizza orders. Think of metadata as the LinkedIn
profile for your data, where it's from.

**Raka Dhar:**
而不是披萨订单。把元数据想象成你数据的LinkedIn个人资料，它来自哪里。

**Raka Dhar:** What it does, and who to call. Today, we will show you
how our tool.

**Raka Dhar:**
它做什么，以及该联系谁。今天，我们将向你展示我们的工具如何。

**Raka Dhar:** Automates metadata generation. Helping streamline
governance, boost.

**Raka Dhar:** 自动化元数据生成。帮助简化治理，提升。

**Raka Dhar:** Transparency, and…. Fast-track our organization's AI
readiness.

**Raka Dhar:** 透明度，并……加速我们组织的AI准备工作。

**Raka Dhar:** This work right now is in pilot phase for easier
understanding, especially for our non-technical audience. We have shared
some key terms and definitions in the chat.

**Raka Dhar:**
这项工作目前处于试点阶段，为了更容易理解，特别是对于我们的非技术观众。我们在聊天中分享了一些关键术语和定义。

**Raka Dhar:** To follow more comfortably. Now, foiling trusted AI with
governed, metadata-rich data.

**Raka Dhar:**
以便更舒适地跟上。现在，用受治理的、富含元数据的数据来支持可信的AI。

**Raka Dhar:** Metadata is one of the building blocks. For data
governance. In an AI-driven world, your first step is not modeling or
building gen AI, it's cleaning up your data closet.

**Raka Dhar:**
元数据是数据治理的基石之一。在AI驱动的世界里，你的第一步不是建模或构建生成式AI，而是清理你的数据仓库。

**Raka Dhar:** To build any intelligent. System. Especially….

**Raka Dhar:** 来构建任何智能系统。特别是……

**Raka Dhar:** Uh, AI-enabled, responsible application, we need a strong
foundation. That starts with data governance.

**Raka Dhar:**
AI赋能的、负责任的应用程序，我们需要一个坚实的基础。这始于数据治理。

**Raka Dhar:** Ensuring data is secure, well-managed, trustworthy across
the organization. You cannot have intelligent, responsible AI without
intelligent data.

**Raka Dhar:**
确保数据在整个组织内是安全的、管理良好的、值得信赖的。没有智能的数据，就不可能有智能的、负责任的AI。

**Raka Dhar:** Governance is your AI's personal trainer. At the heart of
governance is metadata.

**Raka Dhar:** 治理是你AI的私人教练。治理的核心是元数据。

**Raka Dhar:** It provides the context, what your data means, where it
came from, who owns it, and how it should be used.

**Raka Dhar:**
它提供了上下文，你的数据意味着什么，它来自哪里，谁拥有它，以及应该如何使用它。

**Raka Dhar:** To simplify it. Think of metadata as the GPS for your
data.

**Raka Dhar:** 简单来说，把元数据想象成你数据的GPS。

**Raka Dhar:** Without it, your AI is just driving blind. Is like
subtitles for your data.

**Raka Dhar:** 没有它，你的AI就像在盲目驾驶。它就像你数据的字幕。

**Raka Dhar:** It helps everyone understand the story, no matter their
role. And remember, if AI is the engine.

**Raka Dhar:**
它帮助每个人理解故事，无论他们的角色是什么。记住，如果AI是引擎。

**Raka Dhar:** The data governance is the oil. Skip it, and you are
heading for a disaster.

**Raka Dhar:** 数据治理就是机油。跳过它，你就会走向灾难。

**Raka Dhar:** That's exactly where our tool. Metadata generator comes
in, because even the smartest AI cannot go far without a good GPS.

**Raka Dhar:**
这正是我们的工具——元数据生成器——发挥作用的地方，因为即使是最聪明的AI，没有一个好的GPS也走不远。

**Raka Dhar:** So far, I have talked about the importance of data
governance.

**Raka Dhar:** 到目前为止，我谈到了数据治理的重要性。

**Raka Dhar:** And metadata. Now, let's look into this slide. What our
tool does.

**Raka Dhar:** 和元数据。现在，让我们看看这张幻灯片。我们的工具做什么。

**Raka Dhar:** We have built this using Azure-hosted GPT-4. With
enterprise authentication, which makes it flexible enough to work.

**Raka Dhar:**
我们使用Azure托管的GPT-4构建了这个。通过企业认证，使其足够灵活，可以工作。

**Raka Dhar:** Not just with SQL-based system. But also with non-SQL
data sources. One of the key features of our tool is data lineage.

**Raka Dhar:**
不仅与基于SQL的系统，也与非SQL数据源。我们工具的一个关键特性是数据血缘（data
lineage：追踪数据从源头到最终目的地的整个生命周期）。

**Raka Dhar:** It shows how data flows, transforms, and connects across
systems. Think of it as Google Maps.

**Raka Dhar:**
它显示了数据如何在系统间流动、转换和连接。把它想象成谷歌地图。

**Raka Dhar:** For your data pipeline, giving you visibility from source
to destination, and every stop in between.

**Raka Dhar:**
为你的数据管道提供从源头到目的地的可见性，以及中间的每一个站点。

**Raka Dhar:** Now, let's focus on our features. We have, uh, we use AI.

**Raka Dhar:** 现在，让我们关注我们的特性。我们有……我们使用AI。

**Raka Dhar:** To automatically generate plain language descriptions.
For tables, views.

**Raka Dhar:** 自动生成纯语言描述。用于表格、视图。

**Raka Dhar:** And store procedures. This helps breach the gap between
technical metadata.

**Raka Dhar:** 和存储过程。这有助于弥合技术元数据之间的差距。

**Raka Dhar:** And business understanding. Second, we have visualized
data lineage. So that users can see how data flows transform across
system.

**Raka Dhar:**
和业务理解。其次，我们可视化了数据血缘。这样用户就能看到数据流如何在系统间转换。

**Raka Dhar:** We added business contacts. Such as suggested data
quality improvement.

**Raka Dhar:** 我们添加了业务联系人。例如建议的数据质量改进。

**Raka Dhar:** Business term mapping, PHI tagging. To make the metadata
actually useful.

**Raka Dhar:**
业务术语映射，PHI（受保护的健康信息）标记。使元数据真正有用。

**Raka Dhar:** Finally, we offer export options in both JSON and
Markdown. Making it easier to integrate with any tools, documentation,
or data catalog.

**Raka Dhar:**
最后，我们提供JSON和Markdown两种导出选项。使其更容易与任何工具、文档或数据目录集成。

**Raka Dhar:** And all of these features combined. Create a highly
usable, flexible, and intelligent metadata solution.

**Raka Dhar:**
所有这些特性结合起来，创造了一个高度可用、灵活和智能的元数据解决方案。

**Raka Dhar:** Ready for AI governance at scale. Now, my colleague,
Julia, will walk you through.

**Raka Dhar:** 为大规模的AI治理做好准备。现在，我的同事Julia将带你了解。

**Raka Dhar:** How our team previously analyzed metadata. To establish
data lineage.

**Raka Dhar:** 我们的团队以前如何分析元数据来建立数据血缘。

**Raka Dhar:** Followed by a live demonstration of the tool.

**Raka Dhar:** 随后是该工具的现场演示。

**Julia Groza:** Thanks, Raka. So, our team works on a product called
Performance Insights.

**Julia Groza:**
谢谢，Raka。我们的团队正在开发一个名为“性能洞察”的产品。

**Julia Groza:** Which generates analytics for skilled nursing
facilities. Using complex, data-intensive processes.

**Julia Groza:**
它为专业护理机构生成分析报告，使用复杂、数据密集型的流程。

**Julia Groza:** Now, developers working on this product often need to
understand the precise flow of data.

**Julia Groza:** 现在，开发这个产品的开发人员经常需要理解精确的数据流。

**Julia Groza:** By tracing the inputs and outputs for each data table
or stored procedure.

**Julia Groza:** 通过追踪每个数据表或存储过程的输入和输出。

**Julia Groza:** Now, we have high-level documentation of our data flow
process. But before having this tool, it used to be unrealistic to have
detailed step-by-step documentation for every single object.

**Julia Groza:**
现在，我们有我们数据流过程的高层文档。但在拥有这个工具之前，为每一个对象都提供详细的、一步一步的文档是不现实的。

**Julia Groza:** Mapping this data flow can take a developer up to half
a day, costing the company as much as \$1,000 each time.

**Julia Groza:**
映射这个数据流可能需要一个开发人员半天的时间，每次花费公司高达1000美元。

**Julia Groza:** So this manual process highlights the need for better
tools for metadata and data flow analysis.

**Julia Groza:**
所以这个手动过程凸显了对更好的元数据和数据流分析工具的需求。

**Julia Groza:** So now we're going to demo our tool and show how we
made that process much easier.

**Julia Groza:**
所以现在我们将演示我们的工具，并展示我们如何让这个过程变得更容易。

**Julia Groza:** Welcome to the Metadata Generator tool. The first thing
that needs to be done when you're working with this tool is you have to
be connected to a database. So, I'm connected to one of the databases
that we use within our team on Insights.

**Julia Groza:**
欢迎使用元数据生成器工具。使用这个工具时，首先需要连接到数据库。我已经连接到我们团队在Insights上使用的一个数据库。

**Julia Groza:** I'm gonna go to the Database Objects tab, and this is
where all the action happens. So, I have all of the object types.

**Julia Groza:**
我要去数据库对象选项卡，这里是所有操作发生的地方。我这里有所有的对象类型。

**Julia Groza:** That are available in my database. And there's an
option to filter by object type.

**Julia Groza:** 在我的数据库中可用的。还有一个按对象类型筛选的选项。

**Julia Groza:** And I'm gonna generate metadata and talk about. The
descriptions and the data lineage, and how that's being generated within
the tool.

**Julia Groza:**
我将生成元数据并讨论描述和数据血缘，以及它们是如何在工具中生成的。

**Julia Groza:** So, as that's working, the first thing that's happening
is we're getting a plain language description.

**Julia Groza:**
所以，在它工作的时候，首先发生的是我们得到一个纯语言的描述。

**Julia Groza:** Of this object, that will give us information on the
purpose of the table, business context.

**Julia Groza:**
关于这个对象，它将为我们提供关于表的用途、业务背景的信息。

**Julia Groza:** Any relevant tags that could be used later on in
machine learning applications.

**Julia Groza:** 任何相关的标签，这些标签以后可以在机器学习应用中使用。

**Julia Groza:** And other things. So, the way we're getting this is
we're getting all the information about columns, column types.

**Julia Groza:**
以及其他东西。我们获取这个的方式是，我们获取所有关于列、列类型的信息。

**Julia Groza:** Primary keys, foreign keys, indexes, and a little bit
of sample data from the testing environment.

**Julia Groza:** 主键、外键、索引，以及来自测试环境的一点样本数据。

**Julia Groza:** And we're providing that all in a prompt towards the
Azure AI service, and we're getting back that metadata description.

**Julia Groza:** 我们将所有这些信息以提示的形式提供给Azure
AI服务，然后我们得到那个元数据描述。

**Julia Groza:** The second thing that's happening is we're generating a
data flow diagram indicating how data is flowing into and out of this
object.

**Julia Groza:**
第二件事是，我们正在生成一个数据流图，指示数据如何流入和流出这个对象。

**Julia Groza:** You'll see that this information was already generated.
But the way this is working in our tool.

**Julia Groza:**
你会看到这个信息已经生成了。但在我们的工具中，它的工作方式是。

**Julia Groza:** Is we want to find all of the stored procedures, which
are.

**Julia Groza:** 我们想找到所有的存储过程，它们是。

**Julia Groza:** Kind of these scripts that modify data within tables.
And we want to find all those scripts that change, add, or use
information.

**Julia Groza:**
一种修改表中数据的脚本。我们想找到所有那些改变、添加或使用信息的脚本。

**Julia Groza:** In this table. These scripts might also get. Data from
other tables, so we follow all of those connections step-by-step until
we build.

**Julia Groza:**
在这个表中。这些脚本也可能从其他表中获取数据，所以我们一步一步地跟踪所有这些连接，直到我们构建。

**Julia Groza:** This network of database objects that you see here. And
this is called data lineage.

**Julia Groza:** 你在这里看到的这个数据库对象网络。这被称为数据血缘。

**Julia Groza:** And we also look at it the other way around. Not only
do we not… not only do we want to know which data flows into the object
that we selected, which is this table here.

**Julia Groza:**
我们也从另一个角度来看待它。我们不仅想知道哪些数据流入我们选择的对象，也就是这个表。

**Julia Groza:** But we also want to know. How the data from this table
is being used in other objects.

**Julia Groza:**
但我们也想知道这个表中的数据是如何在其他对象中被使用的。

**Julia Groza:** And the way the tool is doing this is it reads all of
the stored procedures, and it finds those source tables and those
destination tables and creates those connections.

**Julia Groza:**
这个工具的做法是，它读取所有的存储过程，找到那些源表和目标表，并创建那些连接。

**Julia Groza:** So, let's look through the metadata that was generated.
We can see that.

**Julia Groza:** 那么，让我们看看生成的元数据。我们可以看到。

**Julia Groza:** Here's the plain language description, kind of giving a
brief overview.

**Julia Groza:** 这是纯语言的描述，给出了一个简要的概述。

**Julia Groza:** Of the table, some business context on why this is
important, those relevant tags I was talking about.

**Julia Groza:**
关于这个表，一些关于它为什么重要的业务背景，以及我之前提到的那些相关标签。

**Julia Groza:** Some data quality checks, and some insights on the
lineage, and some data privacy considerations.

**Julia Groza:**
一些数据质量检查，一些关于血缘的洞察，以及一些数据隐私考虑。

**Julia Groza:** In this lineage graph, it's a little bit small right
now, but I can go back to….

**Julia Groza:** 在这个血缘图中，现在有点小，但我可以回到……

**Julia Groza:** This metadata browser, which shows us. The metadata in
a larger.

**Julia Groza:** 这个元数据浏览器，它向我们展示了更大范围内的元数据。

**Julia Groza:** Context…. Here we go. So this is the same metadata that
we just generated.

**Julia Groza:** 上下文……好了。所以这和我们刚才生成的元数据是一样的。

**Julia Groza:** This will just load in a second. So, here we go.

**Julia Groza:** 这马上就会加载。好了。

**Julia Groza:** So, our selected object is in purple. And our source
tables are in green, and our destination tables are in red.

**Julia Groza:**
所以，我们选择的对象是紫色的。我们的源表是绿色的，我们的目标表是红色的。

**Julia Groza:** And our stored procedures. Or those scripts are in
orange.

**Julia Groza:** 我们的存储过程，或者说那些脚本，是橙色的。

**Julia Groza:** And you can see how data is flowing from this table.

**Julia Groza:** 你可以看到数据是如何从这个表中流出的。

**Julia Groza:** Into this table, and how this table is being used in
all of these destination tables.

**Julia Groza:**
进入这个表，以及这个表是如何在所有这些目标表中被使用的。

**Julia Groza:** And you can start to see how this could take a
developer a really long time to do, but is super quick with our tool.

**Julia Groza:**
你可以开始看到，这可能需要一个开发人员很长时间才能完成，但用我们的工具就超级快。

**Julia Groza:** Now, you might be thinking, how did the tool do this so
quickly? How did it read all these stored procedures and all these
database objects and get that information?

**Julia Groza:**
现在，你可能会想，这个工具怎么能这么快地完成这个？它是如何读取所有这些存储过程和所有这些数据库对象并获取这些信息的？

**Julia Groza:** So when I first started this application and ran it,
there was a background process that was occurring that was reading.

**Julia Groza:**
所以当我第一次启动并运行这个应用程序时，有一个后台进程正在发生，它正在读取。

**Julia Groza:** All of these stored procedure objects. And extracting
the source and destination tables using AI.

**Julia Groza:** 所有这些存储过程对象。并使用AI提取源表和目标表。

**Julia Groza:** And we store all of that information. In our database.
So something really important about this tool is that everything that's
AI-generated.

**Julia Groza:**
我们存储所有这些信息。在我们的数据库中。所以关于这个工具，非常重要的一点是，所有AI生成的东西。

**Julia Groza:** Is then saved in our database. We do this because
excessive calls to the AI service can become time-consuming and costly.
So.

**Julia Groza:**
然后被保存在我们的数据库中。我们这样做是因为对AI服务的过多调用可能会变得耗时且昂贵。所以。

**Julia Groza:** An AI response is only generated once per object, and
then it's reused every time thereafter, because we can have many people.

**Julia Groza:**
每个对象只生成一次AI响应，之后每次都会重复使用，因为我们可以有很多人。

**Julia Groza:** Generating metadata descriptions for the same objects,
and we don't want to make repeated calls.

**Julia Groza:** 为相同的对象生成元数据描述，我们不想进行重复调用。

**Julia Groza:** So you can see that that's indicated by this flag here,
that this metadata is up-to-date.

**Julia Groza:**
所以你可以看到，这里的这个标志表明，这个元数据是最新的。

**Julia Groza:** No regeneration needed. If the database object was
updated, this would be.

**Julia Groza:** 无需重新生成。如果数据库对象被更新，这将是。

**Julia Groza:** Warning you that you should probably regenerate the
metadata. Another thing that I want to share is….

**Julia Groza:** 警告你可能应该重新生成元数据。另一件我想分享的是……

**Julia Groza:** Our…. Ai model specifically looks at column names to
see.

**Julia Groza:** 我们的……AI模型专门查看列名来判断。

**Julia Groza:** If any… there's any PHI, potentially, in these tables.
So, you can see that.

**Julia Groza:**
这些表中是否可能包含任何PHI（受保护的健康信息）。所以，你可以看到。

**Julia Groza:** I selected another table. Um, the metadata description
immediately came up, because this is also saved in the database. We
don't need to generate it again.

**Julia Groza:**
我选择了另一个表。元数据描述立即出现了，因为这也保存在数据库中。我们不需要再次生成它。

**Julia Groza:** And you can see that we might have potential PHI in the
physician first name, middle name, etc.

**Julia Groza:**
你可以看到，我们可能在医生的名字、中间名等方面有潜在的PHI。

**Julia Groza:** And the user should be aware of this. The second thing
I want to show you with this tool is our schema comparison feature.

**Julia Groza:**
用户应该意识到这一点。我想向你展示的这个工具的第二个功能是我们的模式比较功能。

**Julia Groza:** Now, the purpose of this feature is. If you're working
with multiple database objects, and you want to understand the
difference between them, whether it be structure-wise or business
context-wise.

**Julia Groza:**
现在，这个功能的目的是。如果你正在处理多个数据库对象，并且你想了解它们之间的差异，无论是结构上还是业务背景上。

**Julia Groza:** It's helpful to be able to compare them. So, I'm gonna
pick two schemas, and when I'm picking two schemas.

**Julia Groza:**
能够比较它们是很有帮助的。所以，我准备选择两个模式，当我选择两个模式时。

**Julia Groza:** The tool is finding all of the common objects between
them that can be compared.

**Julia Groza:** 该工具正在查找它们之间所有可以比较的共同对象。

**Julia Groza:** And it's doing this based on naming conventions. So, as
you can see here.

**Julia Groza:** 它是基于命名约定来做的。所以，正如你在这里看到的。

**Julia Groza:** Um, these two object names…. Are similar to each other,
except for that schema.

**Julia Groza:** 这两个对象名……彼此相似，除了那个模式。

**Julia Groza:** Name difference. So when I go ahead and compare
schemas…. This is already saved to the database as well, like I
mentioned, we save all the responses in the database.

**Julia Groza:**
名称差异。所以当我继续比较模式时……这也已经保存到数据库中了，正如我提到的，我们把所有的响应都保存在数据库中。

**Julia Groza:** We get a summary of differences on the parameters, the
objects used within this.

**Julia Groza:** 我们得到了关于参数、其中使用的对象的差异摘要。

**Julia Groza:** Particular object, any differences in logic. I'll put
columns, as well as some risks and recommendations for working with
these.

**Julia Groza:**
特定对象，任何逻辑上的差异。我会列出列，以及一些使用这些对象的风险和建议。

**Julia Groza:** Two objects. So, overall, this tool is very helpful for
developers to get better business context on database objects.

**Julia Groza:**
两个对象。所以，总的来说，这个工具对开发人员更好地了解数据库对象的业务背景非常有帮助。

**Julia Groza:** It's preparing the data, giving it relevant tags that
could be used later on in those machine learning applications.

**Julia Groza:**
它正在准备数据，给它相关的标签，这些标签以后可以在那些机器学习应用中使用。

**Julia Groza:** And the most important thing is it's developing that
data lineage and showing that data flow.

**Julia Groza:** 最重要的是，它正在开发数据血缘并展示数据流。

**Julia Groza:** Which is imperative when you're building on top of or
modifying your data flow transformation.

**Julia Groza:** 当你在构建或修改你的数据流转换时，这是至关重要的。

**Julia Groza:** Welcome to….

**Julia Groza:** 欢迎来到……

**Julia Groza:** Okay. Uh, so…. Based on the database that was demoed in
that video, which is specific to.

**Julia Groza:** 好的。所以……基于那个视频中演示的数据库，它是特定于。

**Julia Groza:** Our product, Performance Insights. Um, that database
has roughly 1,000 database objects.

**Julia Groza:**
我们的产品，性能洞察。那个数据库大约有1000个数据库对象。

**Julia Groza:** So, this tool has the potential to save. 250 to 4,000
hours in developer time.

**Julia Groza:** 所以，这个工具有潜力节省250到4000小时的开发人员时间。

**Julia Groza:** And \$60,000 to a million dollars in cost savings. And
again, this is just for one database for insights alone.

**Julia Groza:**
并节省6万到100万美元的成本。再次强调，这仅仅是针对一个洞察数据库。

**Julia Groza:** So, our goal with this tool is to make this tool
available to all engineering teams.

**Julia Groza:**
所以，我们这个工具的目标是让所有工程团队都能使用这个工具。

**Julia Groza:** For their respective databases. So everyone can benefit
from the same time and cost savings.

**Julia Groza:**
为他们各自的数据库。这样每个人都能从同样的时间和成本节省中受益。

**Julia Groza:** Uh, and for our non-engineering teams, we hope we
provided another example that you can take away from this symposium.

**Julia Groza:**
对于我们的非工程团队，我们希望我们提供了另一个例子，你们可以从这次研讨会中带走。

**Julia Groza:** On how to break down complex, repetitive workflows. And
use AI for well-defined steps along the way.

**Julia Groza:**
关于如何分解复杂、重复的工作流程，并在过程中使用AI来完成定义明确的步骤。

**Julia Groza:** Now, we have several planned enhancements to make this
tool even more valuable.

**Julia Groza:**
现在，我们有几个计划中的增强功能，以使这个工具更有价值。

**Julia Groza:** The first one is that we want to increase the
granularity of that data lineage graph.

**Julia Groza:** 第一个是，我们想增加那个数据血缘图的粒度。

**Julia Groza:** So right now, it's tracking the data flow across
tables. But we want to make it track the data flow across columns. So
this is going to give developers better visibility into how changes to
individual columns.

**Julia Groza:**
所以现在，它正在跟踪跨表的数据流。但我们想让它跟踪跨列的数据流。这将让开发人员更好地了解单个列的更改如何。

**Julia Groza:** Can impact the entire system. Next, we want to improve
our metadata itself.

**Julia Groza:** 影响整个系统。接下来，我们想改进我们的元数据本身。

**Julia Groza:** And divide it into business, technical, and operational
metadata. So it's more actionable for different types of users.

**Julia Groza:**
并将其分为业务、技术和运营元数据。这样对不同类型的用户来说更具可操作性。

**Julia Groza:** And finally, we want to expand even the reach of this
tool beyond databases.

**Julia Groza:** 最后，我们甚至想将这个工具的范围扩展到数据库之外。

**Julia Groza:** We'd love for this tool to be able to document the data
flow for any kind of repository that has some kind of data flow, which
is a lot of repositories.

**Julia Groza:**
我们希望这个工具能够为任何有数据流的知识库记录数据流，而这样的知识库有很多。

**Julia Groza:** When it comes to responsible AI. The most important
part of our project is that we're saving every AI-generated result.

**Julia Groza:**
当谈到负责任的AI时。我们项目最重要的部分是，我们保存每一个AI生成的结果。

**Julia Groza:** With timestamps, enabling full review and auditability.
And when we do prompt the Azure AI service, we're creating highly
specific, context-rich prompts.

**Julia Groza:** 带有时间戳，实现全面的审查和可审计性。当我们提示Azure
AI服务时，我们正在创建高度具体、上下文丰富的提示。

**Julia Groza:** With standardized inputs and standardized outputs,
allowing us to control the generated response as much as we can.

**Julia Groza:**
通过标准化的输入和标准化的输出，让我们能尽可能地控制生成的响应。

**Julia Groza:** But most of the logic in this tool is handled by
deterministic code that us as developers can review.

**Julia Groza:**
但这个工具中的大部分逻辑是由我们作为开发人员可以审查的确定性代码处理的。

**Julia Groza:** So, after completing this project, we have two key
takeaways. One is that AI is most effective when you have a strong
understanding of what it's generating.

**Julia Groza:**
所以，在完成这个项目后，我们有两个关键的收获。一个是，当你对AI生成的内容有深刻的理解时，AI是最有效的。

**Julia Groza:** It's easy to rely on AI suggestions without grasping
the underlying libraries in your code, for example.

**Julia Groza:** 很容易依赖AI的建议，而没有掌握你代码中底层的库，例如。

**Julia Groza:** But we found that reviewing documentation and then
guiding the AI ultimately saved us more time than prompting it without
sufficient context.

**Julia Groza:**
但我们发现，审查文档然后指导AI，最终比在没有足够上下文的情况下提示它节省了我们更多的时间。

**Julia Groza:** And lastly, I keep talking about this point, but we
found that AI works best for small, well-defined tasks, because it
allows us to maintain control.

**Julia Groza:**
最后，我一直在谈论这一点，但我们发现AI最适合处理小的、定义明确的任务，因为它让我们能保持控制。

**Julia Groza:** And validate results as we go. So, thank you so much
for attending this demo, and thank you to the AI Symposium team for
giving us the opportunity to share this with all of you.

**Julia Groza:**
并在过程中验证结果。所以，非常感谢你们参加这次演示，也感谢AI研讨会团队给我们机会与大家分享这个。

**Julia Groza:** And we can take any other questions that you have.
Thank you.

**Julia Groza:** 我们可以回答你们提出的任何其他问题。谢谢。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Box full of scraps. You've got Wi-Fi and Copilot,
so no excuses.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 一箱废料。你有了Wi-Fi和Copilot，所以没有借口。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Oh my god, I love that! So, does anyone use this,

**Ketki Yennemadi:**
天哪，我喜欢这个！那么，有人用这种类型的提示吗？你知道，你可以出于各种原因使用这种类型的提示。实际上，我经常使用这个。我让AI扮演不同的角色。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** And help me practice, uh, typically for

**Ketki Yennemadi:**

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Because then, it'll offer more targeted critique

**Ketki Yennemadi:**

**Ketki Yennemadi:**

### 用例11：Kate Kaplya - 利用Copilot分析实施指标

**Kate Kaplya:** All right. Sounds good. Let me go ahead and start
sharing my screen.

**Kate Kaplya:** 你刚才吓到我了。我就想，我是不是走错地方了？

**Ketki Yennemadi:** I'm so sorry about that.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 我非常抱歉。

**Kate Kaplya:** No, it's okay. All good, all good. Can everyone see my

**Kate Kaplya:**
不，没关系。一切都好，一切都好。大家现在能看到我的屏幕吗？

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 是的，我们可以。

**Kate Kaplya:** Okay, wonderful. So, good afternoon, everyone. My name
is Kay Calia, and I'm an implementation consultant.

**Kate Kaplya:** 好的，太棒了。大家下午好。我叫Kay

**Kate Kaplya:** Uh, with the pharmacy and integrated medication
management team. My presentation today will be focused on leveraging
Microsoft 365 Copilot app.

**Kate Kaplya:**
我来自药房和综合药物管理团队。我今天的演讲将重点介绍如何利用Microsoft
365 Copilot应用程序。

**Kate Kaplya:** To analyze Pulse implementation clinical metrics for
facilities implementing point-click care solutions.

**Kate Kaplya:**
来分析实施PointClickCare解决方案的设施的Pulse实施临床指标。

**Kate Kaplya:** This use case is currently in the pilot stage, and
previously it's been reviewed with the consultant team, as well as I've
used it on my own projects.

**Kate Kaplya:**
这个用例目前处于试点阶段，之前已经与顾问团队进行了审查，我也在自己的项目中使用过它。

**Kate Kaplya:** So as part of the project lifecycle, consultants are
preparing a post-implementation metrics Excel dashboard.

**Kate Kaplya:**
作为项目生命周期的一部分，顾问们正在准备一个实施后指标的Excel仪表盘。

**Kate Kaplya:** Using the data pulled from production self-service
portal. Typically, this is done over a 4-week period, where we meet with
customers to review and discuss the current health status of their
database, and to identify improvements.

**Kate Kaplya:**
使用从生产自助服务门户提取的数据。通常，这会在一个为期4周的时间内完成，我们会与客户会面，审查和讨论他们数据库的当前健康状况，并确定改进之处。

**Kate Kaplya:** So, consultants spend time not only generating reports,
but also validating the data in advance to create action plans.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以，顾问们不仅花时间生成报告，还提前验证数据以制定行动计划。

**Kate Kaplya:** And this idea came to me back in February during a
cross-functional project manager and consultant onsite.

**Kate Kaplya:**
这个想法是在二月份，在一次跨职能的项目经理和顾问现场会议上产生的。

**Kate Kaplya:** Where we discuss how AI can be incorporated into the
implementation lifecycle.

**Kate Kaplya:** 我们讨论了如何将AI融入实施生命周期。

**Kate Kaplya:** I found that I frequently spend a lot of time reviewing
the metrics report, developing personalized recommendations, and
preparing for monitoring calls.

**Kate Kaplya:**
我发现我经常花很多时间审查指标报告，制定个性化建议，并为监控电话做准备。

**Kate Kaplya:** So today, I would like to show you how Copilot can be
leveraged to extract performance indicators and generally tailored
action plans from the metrics report.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以今天，我想向你展示如何利用Copilot从指标报告中提取性能指标并生成量身定制的行动计划。

**Kate Kaplya:** For the demonstration, I'm using a pre-built test
clinical dashboard containing data for two facilities. The dashboard
contains five different clinical workflows, which in turn contain
multiple metrics listed on the left.

**Kate Kaplya:**
为了演示，我正在使用一个预先构建的测试临床仪表盘，其中包含两个设施的数据。该仪表盘包含五个不同的临床工作流程，每个工作流程又包含左侧列出的多个指标。

**Kate Kaplya:** Displaying data over 4 weeks. One thing to note about
the dashboard is that it contains macro elements, which Copilot is
unable to analyze, so must be converted to a regular Excel workbook
before running the analysis.

**Kate Kaplya:**
显示4周的数据。关于这个仪表盘，需要注意的一点是，它包含宏元素，Copilot无法分析，所以在运行分析之前必须将其转换为常规的Excel工作簿。

**Kate Kaplya:** The demo will review how to transform a prepared
metrics report into meaningful, facility-specific improvement
strategies.

**Kate Kaplya:**
演示将回顾如何将准备好的指标报告转化为有意义的、针对特定设施的改进策略。

**Kate Kaplya:** Enhancing care quality, compliance, and operational
efficiency.

**Kate Kaplya:** 提高护理质量、合规性和运营效率。

**Kate Kaplya:** For the purpose of this demonstration, I've already
entered my prompt.

**Kate Kaplya:** 为了这次演示，我已经输入了我的提示。

**Kate Kaplya:** And I've already attached the workbook.

**Kate Kaplya:** 我已经附上了工作簿。

**Kate Kaplya:** I'm not sure what happened.

**Kate Kaplya:** 我不确定发生了什么。

**Kate Kaplya:** Get to this prompt in order for the analysis to
complete, as it can take some time, depending on the number of
facilities that you have.

**Kate Kaplya:**
为了完成分析，需要进入这个提示，因为这可能需要一些时间，具体取决于你拥有的设施数量。

**Kate Kaplya:** The number of weeks of data that you have. But you can

**Kate Kaplya:**
你拥有的数据周数。但你可以保存你的提示，或者你可以输入你的提示。

**Kate Kaplya:** Under View Prompts within your chat. You can look at
the prompt gallery, and I've saved my prompt under your prompts.

**Kate Kaplya:**
在你的聊天中的“查看提示”下。你可以查看提示库，我把我的提示保存在了“你的提示”下。

**Kate Kaplya:** And select your specific prompt. And in this prompt,
I've outlined.

**Kate Kaplya:** 并选择你的特定提示。在这个提示中，我概述了。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, some details about the request. So I've asked

**Kate Kaplya:** 关于请求的一些细节。所以我请Copilot为每一个……

**Kate Kaplya:** Clinical workflow, um, separated by facility with
specific focus areas, next steps.

**Kate Kaplya:**
临床工作流程，按设施分开，有特定的重点领域和下一步措施。

**Kate Kaplya:**

**Kate Kaplya:** 这份报告和分析是基于我将要附加的Pulse实施货币指标文件。

**Kate Kaplya:** I've also asked it to highlight promising trends for
each workflow, including multiple metrics, and also separating by

**Kate Kaplya:**

**Kate Kaplya:** So although Ability sent my prompt, in order to

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以虽然Ability发送了我的提示，但为了实际添加附件，我会去点击这里。

**Kate Kaplya:** And add content. And then I can search for my specific

**Kate Kaplya:** 并添加内容。然后我可以搜索我的特定内容。

**Kate Kaplya:** Or I can upload it from device or attach cloud file, so
if I typed in a workbook.

**Kate Kaplya:**
或者我可以从设备上传或附加云文件，所以如果我输入一个工作簿。

**Kate Kaplya:** I can find my workbook in here as well. But as I've
already included my document in here.

**Kate Kaplya:**
我也可以在这里找到我的工作簿。但因为我已经在这里包含了我的文档。

**Kate Kaplya:** I can go ahead and just remove the prompt. Because I've
already sent the prompt in here.

**Kate Kaplya:** 我可以继续并删除这个提示。因为我已经在这里发送了提示。

**Kate Kaplya:** And then I'll be able to review the analysis generated
by Copilot.

**Kate Kaplya:** 然后我就能审查Copilot生成的分析了。

**Kate Kaplya:** Down here, um, Copilot analyzed the report that was
uploaded and provided me with the following information.

**Kate Kaplya:** 在这里，Copilot分析了上传的报告，并为我提供了以下信息。

**Kate Kaplya:** So, it included…. The details per facility, and it also
split it up into different workflows.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以，它包括了……每个设施的详细信息，并且还将其分成了不同的工作流程。

**Kate Kaplya:** It's outlining promising trends as requested, any focus
areas, so any areas that I've noticed maybe the numbers are higher in,
or maybe there's uncleared items, as outlined in here.

**Kate Kaplya:**
它按要求概述了有希望的趋势，任何重点领域，所以任何我注意到数字可能更高，或者可能有未清理项目的领域，都在这里概述了。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, any next steps, as well as recommended resources.
As we can see, it's separating by those workflows, so we have
interdisciplinary admission, medication management dashboards.

**Kate Kaplya:**
任何下一步措施，以及推荐的资源。正如我们所看到的，它按那些工作流程分开，所以我们有跨学科入院、药物管理仪表盘。

**Kate Kaplya:** Orders portal, any focus areas. And then medication
management pharmacy Orders Portal, and that was for my first facility.

**Kate Kaplya:**
订单门户，任何重点领域。然后是药物管理药房订单门户，那是我第一个设施的。

**Kate Kaplya:** And then I have the same information for that second
facility.

**Kate Kaplya:** 然后我有了第二个设施的同样信息。

**Kate Kaplya:** Promise and Trends, focus areas, next steps, and then
recommended resources.

**Kate Kaplya:** 承诺与趋势、重点领域、下一步措施，然后是推荐资源。

**Kate Kaplya:** And we can scroll down. And review all of that
information that was outlined.

**Kate Kaplya:** 我们可以向下滚动，并审查所有概述的信息。

**Kate Kaplya:** Per facility, and it asked me if I want to generate a
formatted document, or if I want to create a slide deck.

**Kate Kaplya:**
每个设施，它问我是否想生成一个格式化的文档，或者是否想创建一个幻灯片。

**Kate Kaplya:** So, as you can see, this analysis allows consultants to
prepare for the metrics review call.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以，正如你所看到的，这个分析让顾问们能够为指标审查电话会议做准备。

**Kate Kaplya:** And to, um, discuss what the facility can improve on,
or maybe to highlight any areas where a facility has been doing well, or
where a facility has been improving.

**Kate Kaplya:**
并讨论设施可以改进的地方，或者突出显示设施做得好的地方，或者设施正在改进的地方。

**Kate Kaplya:** So all of the information was already generated by
Copilot. And it also included some recommended resources, um, any
required next steps.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以所有的信息都已经被Copilot生成了。它还包括了一些推荐的资源，以及任何需要的下一步措施。

**Kate Kaplya:** So any actions that the facility should be taking. Um,
so that information can also be shared with the facility on the call.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以设施应该采取的任何行动。这些信息也可以在通话中与设施分享。

**Kate Kaplya:** And something that can be included in a follow-up email
or further conversation with the facility, um, those action items can be
outlined.

**Kate Kaplya:**
并且可以包含在后续邮件或与设施的进一步对话中，那些行动项可以被概述。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, as you're discussing, um, any improvement areas or
any action items with the facility.

**Kate Kaplya:** 当你与设施讨论任何改进领域或任何行动项时。

**Kate Kaplya:** All right, so you can also request Copilot to summarize
key points for high-level overview, or to request a more detailed
breakdown for a specific workflow.

**Kate Kaplya:**
好的，所以你也可以请求Copilot总结关键点以进行高层概览，或者请求对特定工作流程进行更详细的分解。

**Kate Kaplya:** So on this slide, I included a quick visual of the
input versus analysis. So on the left, we have the clinical dashboard
metrics data, and then on the right, we have the tailored action plan
generated by Copilot.

**Kate Kaplya:**
在这张幻灯片上，我包含了一个输入与分析的快速视觉对比。左边是临床仪表盘指标数据，右边是Copilot生成的量身定制的行动计划。

**Kate Kaplya:** So why is this use case important? Um, in terms of
impact, we're looking at increased consultant efficiency when preparing
post-goal life recommendations.

**Kate Kaplya:**
那么为什么这个用例很重要呢？在影响方面，我们看到在准备实施后建议时，顾问的效率提高了。

**Kate Kaplya:** Consultants can reclaim time, saving up to 20% of an
8-hour workday when preparing metrics for four facilities daily.

**Kate Kaplya:**
顾问们可以节省时间，每天为四个设施准备指标时，可以节省高达8小时工作日的20%。

**Kate Kaplya:** We also have standardized improvement planning across
facilities, allowing for continuous workflow optimization.

**Kate Kaplya:**
我们还在所有设施中标准化了改进规划，从而实现了持续的工作流程优化。

**Kate Kaplya:** And last but not least, this empowers implementation
team with actionable insights and direct access to support materials.

**Kate Kaplya:**
最后但同样重要的是，这为实施团队提供了可操作的洞察和直接访问支持材料的途径。

**Kate Kaplya:** Leading to increased productivity and capacity to
process three times more facilities in the same amount of time.

**Kate Kaplya:** 从而提高了生产力，并能在相同时间内处理三倍多的设施。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, in terms of lessons learned, uh, you do want to
make sure to use very specific and detailed prompts outlining what
information to analyze.

**Kate Kaplya:**
在经验教训方面，你确实要确保使用非常具体和详细的提示，概述要分析什么信息。

**Kate Kaplya:** Including, but not limited to, facility and workflow
needs names or specific metrics.

**Kate Kaplya:** 包括但不限于设施和工作流程的名称或特定指标。

**Kate Kaplya:** And, um, linking metrics to resources was also
identified as an area of improvement, um, as Copilot was unable to
extract resources directly stored within the customer support portal.
For example, it is possible to pull in smart zone eCourses, however,
that information was only pulled from the documents that were found in
Shared Workspaces.

**Kate Kaplya:**
而且，将指标与资源链接也被确定为一个改进领域，因为Copilot无法直接从客户支持门户中提取资源。例如，可以提取智能区域的电子课程，但这些信息只从共享工作区中找到的文档中提取。

**Kate Kaplya:** It also may pull personal cloud files and email
attachments from my experience.

**Kate Kaplya:** 根据我的经验，它也可能提取个人云文件和邮件附件。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, resources and recommendations need detailed review
to confirm that they apply to the facility-specific workflows. For
example, you want to take into account differences between the skilled
nursing facility versus an assisted living facility.

**Kate Kaplya:**
资源和建议需要详细审查，以确认它们适用于特定设施的工作流程。例如，你需要考虑到专业护理机构和辅助生活机构之间的差异。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, how it kind of help others. Uh, point-click here,
so by linking metrics to specific how-to guides and resources, AI acts
as a dynamic navigator, bridging data and resources.

**Kate Kaplya:**
它如何能帮助他人。在这里，通过将指标与特定的操作指南和资源链接起来，AI扮演了一个动态导航员的角色，连接了数据和资源。

**Kate Kaplya:** Which in turn reduces training gaps and improves
adoption. Different prompts can be utilized to access training resources
and recommendations for learning and development in customer support
teams.

**Kate Kaplya:**
这反过来又减少了培训差距并提高了采用率。可以利用不同的提示来访问培训资源和客户支持团队学习与发展的建议。

**Kate Kaplya:** And it also accelerates post-school life monitoring, so
co-pilots can automate that first layer of post-go-life review.

**Kate Kaplya:**
它还加速了实施后的监控，所以Copilot可以自动化实施后审查的第一层。

**Kate Kaplya:** Flagging trends and surfacing support materials. And
this model can be replicated across other workflows, such as billing for
implementation, customer success, and account management teams.

**Kate Kaplya:**
标记趋势并提供支持材料。这个模型可以复制到其他工作流程中，比如实施、客户成功和客户管理团队的计费。

**Kate Kaplya:** Uh, for responsible use of AI, you do want to make sure
to validate the recommendations against facility-specific nuances.

**Kate Kaplya:**
为了负责任地使用AI，你确实要确保根据特定设施的细微差别来验证建议。

**Kate Kaplya:** So you want to approve, edit, or annotate the plan
before actually sharing it with the facility.

**Kate Kaplya:**
所以在实际与设施分享之前，你想要批准、编辑或注释这个计划。

**Kate Kaplya:** And you also want to review the reference sources to
check for PHI or project data, specifically focusing on items that are
used by Copilot to generate recommendations and supporting materials.

**Kate Kaplya:**
你还想审查参考来源，以检查是否存在PHI（受保护的健康信息）或项目数据，特别关注Copilot用于生成建议和支持材料的项目。

**Kate Kaplya:** And finally, you want to refine your AI prompts or
adjust your metric thresholds based on the generate responses.

**Kate Kaplya:**
最后，你想要根据生成的响应来优化你的AI提示或调整你的指标阈值。

**Kate Kaplya:** As risk thresholds may vary from project to project.
Um, in conclusion, this use case allows to reduce the amount of time
spent on analyzing metrics to prepare for monitoring sessions.

**Kate Kaplya:**
因为风险阈值可能因项目而异。总而言之，这个用例可以减少分析指标以准备监控会议所花费的时间。

**Kate Kaplya:** Freeing up time for strategic outreach. It also shows
how AI can transform raw post-implementation data into actionable
insights.

**Kate Kaplya:**
从而腾出时间进行战略性外展。它还展示了AI如何能将原始的实施后数据转化为可操作的洞察。

**Kate Kaplya:** Um, enabling teams to make faster evidence-based
decisions without the manual analysis.

**Kate Kaplya:**
使团队能够在没有手动分析的情况下，更快地做出基于证据的决策。

**Kate Kaplya:** Which ensures more efficient reviews, improved care
outcomes, and a future-ready approach to continuous improvement.

**Kate Kaplya:**
这确保了更高效的审查、改善的护理成果，以及一个面向未来的持续改进方法。

### 主持人互动：AI解释政策

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Okay, perfect. I'm going to drop this in. All
right, so, while we wait for our next presenters to get set up.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
好的，完美。我把这个放进去。好的，那么，在我们等待下一位演讲者准备的时候。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** I want you to use Copilot on a web browser and
enter the following prompt. I've also dropped it in the chat.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
我希望你在网页浏览器上使用Copilot并输入以下提示。我也把它放到了聊天里。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Ask Copilot to explain the acceptable use
policy as if. Your 12th. Highlight key things that you need to be aware
of to ensure that you meet acceptable use, and then once you've gotten a
response, drop an emoji in the chat.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
让Copilot像对12岁的孩子一样解释可接受使用政策。突出你需要注意的关键事项，以确保你符合可接受使用，然后一旦你得到回应，在聊天中发一个表情符号。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** On your reaction for what you got. Uh, so when
I did this, I was actually really surprised. It did a really good job of
breaking down the policy and language that was really simple to
understand.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
关于你得到的回应。当我这么做的时候，我真的非常惊讶。它把政策和语言分解得非常好，非常容易理解。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** It linked it back to school, which makes sense
for our 12-year-old.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
它把它和学校联系起来，这对我们12岁的孩子来说很有意义。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 而且它确实很好地突出了我需要注意的关键事项。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
来大致了解政策的内容，或者之后，特别是如果有一个部分你不太理解，这可能是一个好方法。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
让它从不同的受众角度告诉你。我在日常生活中也使用类似的提示。通常，当我试图学习新东西时。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Or, if I'm trying to explain something

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 他会问我一些问题，比如，雨是从哪里来的？

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
我正试图向一个5岁的孩子解释，所以我会把它放到Copilot里说。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Ruben Vieira:**

**Ruben Vieira:**

**Ruben Vieira:** 提问，与Pharmacy GPT互动，以获取所需信息。

**Ruben Vieira:** 所以他们就是进入Pharmacy GPT，提出问题。

**Ruben Vieira:**

**Ruben Vieira:** 它的答案。然后它会立即发送回用户。

**Ruben Vieira:** Uh, and now back to you, Syed.

**Syed Hasan:** All right, so… so as Ruben mentioned, um….

**Syed Hasan:** 好的，所以……正如Ruben提到的……

**Syed Hasan:** Agents are really only as good as what you train them

**Syed Hasan:** 智能体的优劣完全取决于你用什么来训练它们。

**Syed Hasan:** Um, so we had to really figure out a quick way of

**Syed Hasan:** 所以我们必须找到一种快速生成的方法。

**Syed Hasan:** Documentation that everybody loves, right? Documentation
is the beta of everyone's existence here. Uh, so we… we did unlock a
path here to.

**Syed Hasan:**
每个人都喜欢的文档，对吧？文档是这里每个人存在的测试版。所以我们……我们确实在这里解锁了一条通往……

**Syed Hasan:** Quick, detailed, and accurate documentation. Uh, so

**Syed Hasan:**
快速、详细、准确的文档。基本上，我们做的是，对于每一个发布，我们都确定我们的可交付成果。

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:** Uh, generally, you would find yourself being able to

type.

**Syed Hasan:**
通常，你会发现自己能在15分钟内讲完一件需要你花5个小时打字的事情。

**Syed Hasan:**
所以我们去获取我们的转录稿，然后把转录稿反馈给Copilot，并从中构建详细的文档。

**Syed Hasan:** Um, so going from feature intent to feature logic to

**Syed Hasan:** 从功能意图到功能逻辑，再到市场营销、销售话术。

**Syed Hasan:** To training checklists, internal training checklists,

**Syed Hasan:**
到培训清单、内部培训清单、外部培训清单、课程大纲，无论是什么情况。

**Syed Hasan:** We can actually get that in a matter of minutes using
Copilot. And when I talk about detailed, um.

**Syed Hasan:**
我们实际上可以在几分钟内使用Copilot得到这些。当我谈到详细的……

**Syed Hasan:** Documentation, I mean detailed documentation. These
are….

**Syed Hasan:** 文档，我指的是详细的文档。这些是……

**Syed Hasan:** 10 to 15 to 20 page documents on a single feature.

**Syed Hasan:** 关于单个功能的10到15到20页的文档。

**Syed Hasan:** Right, so it's very detailed. And complete
documentation. We then go, um, and update our data dictionary. So we had
to build data dictionaries, because while.

**Syed Hasan:**
对，所以它非常详细。而且是完整的文档。然后我们去更新我们的数据字典。所以我们必须构建数据字典，因为虽然。

**Syed Hasan:** You may have heard a lot today that. You know, your
responses are only as good as the prompt. We kind of wanted to make that
process a little bit easier for people, so that people can talk to it in
a human way.

**Syed Hasan:**
你今天可能听到了很多。你知道，你的回应只和你的提示一样好。我们想让这个过程对人们来说更容易一些，这样人们就可以用人类的方式和它交谈。

**Syed Hasan:** So we have built data dictionaries where we have
documented abbreviations or similar terms that people may use to refer
to certain things, so….

**Syed Hasan:**
所以我们构建了数据字典，在其中记录了人们可能用来指代某些事物的缩写或类似术语，所以……

**Syed Hasan:** Quick example would be a facility. Uh, depending on
which side of the market you're dealing with, they may be called skilled
nursing facilities, or they may be called assisted living facilities, or

**Syed Hasan:**
一个快速的例子是设施。根据你所处理的市场方面，它们可能被称为专业护理机构，或者辅助生活机构，或者可能简单地被称为家。

**Syed Hasan:** Right? Uh, so we built these data dictionaries, so we
update them if they are needed.

**Syed Hasan:**
对吧？所以我们构建了这些数据字典，如果需要的话，我们会更新它们。

**Syed Hasan:** And then we go ahead and train pharmacy GPT with that
same documentation.

**Syed Hasan:** 然后我们继续用同样的文档来训练Pharmacy GPT。

**Syed Hasan:** Um, and test it. So really, all we're doing here is
we're using AI.

**Syed Hasan:** 并测试它。所以实际上，我们在这里做的就是使用AI。

**Syed Hasan:** Degenerate content to feed back to the AI. Right? So
that's really the process here. And I'll just give you guys a quick look
into what I mean by detailed documentation. So this is just one of the

**Syed Hasan:**
生成内容以反馈给AI。对吧？所以这才是这里的真正过程。我这就让你们快速看一下我所说的详细文档是什么意思。这只是我们创建的众多文档之一。

**Syed Hasan:** Um, you can see this is an 11-page document, a monster
of a document with… with bunch and bunch of details captured in here,
extremely knowledge-rich.

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:** Right, and this is 95% of what you see on my screen is

**Syed Hasan:** 对，你屏幕上看到的95%都是Copilot生成的。

**Syed Hasan:** Right, so we've got a bunch of these documents that
we've been creating, so if anybody needs any help with how we're doing
this, feel free to reach out, and we'll be more than happy to help.

**Syed Hasan:**
对，所以我们已经创建了一堆这样的文档，所以如果有人需要关于我们如何做的帮助，请随时联系，我们非常乐意提供帮助。

**Syed Hasan:** So… so as soon as we are data-focused. The big thing for
us was, how do we become responsible with our use of AI? Well, number
one, again.

**Syed Hasan:**
所以……一旦我们以数据为中心。对我们来说，最重要的事情是，我们如何能负责任地使用AI？嗯，第一，再次。

**Syed Hasan:** Ai is, yeah, it can hallucinate, so one of the things
we've done is all of our responses will always cite the source materials

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:**

**Syed Hasan:**

### 用例13：Jennifer Magana, Maja Madirazza, Krisika Suthan & Charley Yang - Figma与Copilot在UX设计中的应用

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Yeah, thanks everyone. Hi, uh, Charlie,
Maya, Krisika, and I from User Research and Design are excited to share.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
是的，谢谢大家。嗨，我是用户研究与设计部的Charlie、Maya、Krisika和我，我们很高兴能分享。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** How we're partnering with AI to help us
move faster, spot insights sooner, and make our work more inclusive.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
我们如何与AI合作，以帮助我们更快地行动，更早地发现洞察，并使我们的工作更具包容性。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** So let's get started. Um, today we're
focusing on that early phase of product development.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
那么让我们开始吧。今天我们关注的是产品开发的早期阶段。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** When we're still figuring out what to
build, it's what we call product discovery.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
当我们还在弄清楚要构建什么时，我们称之为产品发现。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** This phase is often overwhelming. Ideas
are slow to form. Research findings are shared too late, and
collaboration happens, but in silos.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
这个阶段通常是压倒性的。想法形成缓慢。研究发现分享得太晚，协作虽然发生，但却是孤立的。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** That's why we're rethinking how we
explore and align. We're learning how to partner with our AI tools we
call Design Pals.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
这就是为什么我们正在重新思考我们如何探索和协调。我们正在学习如何与我们称之为“设计伙伴”的AI工具合作。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** To change how we collaborate and build
with more confidence. We each give it a role to play.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
来改变我们的协作方式，并更有信心地进行构建。我们每个人都给它分配一个角色。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Maya will showcase her ideation coach.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:** Maya将展示她的构思教练。

**Maja Madirazza:** Sigma Make is our new AI-powered ideation coach. It
helps us remix ideas quickly and explore multiple design directions to
solve user problems.

**Maja Madirazza:** Figma
Make是我们新的AI驱动的构思教练。它帮助我们快速重组想法，并探索多种设计方向来解决用户问题。

**Maja Madirazza:** I recently used it to explore how users could
indicate the location of documentation within an assessment.

**Maja Madirazza:** 我最近用它来探索用户如何在评估中指示文档的位置。

**Maja Madirazza:** Instead of sketching, I use prompts to generate a
design that closely matched what I had in mind.

**Maja Madirazza:**
我没有画草图，而是使用提示来生成一个与我心中所想非常匹配的设计。

**Maja Madirazza:** Being the design helped me uncover a new challenge.
How might we help users not just select a progress note, but select the
right one?

**Maja Madirazza:**
这个设计帮助我发现了一个新挑战。我们如何能帮助用户不仅是选择一个进度笔记，而是选择正确的那个？

**Maja Madirazza:** So for the next round, I adjusted the prompt to
include more context, like, who wrote the note.

**Maja Madirazza:**
所以在下一轮，我调整了提示，加入了更多的上下文，比如，谁写的笔记。

**Maja Madirazza:** Their role, and the date. Then I realized, wouldn't
it be better if users could actually preview the entire node before
selecting it?

**Maja Madirazza:**
他们的角色和日期。然后我意识到，如果用户在选择之前能实际预览整个笔记，会不会更好？

**Maja Madirazza:** I then added a preview feature. Now, when users
click preview, the note expands, allowing.

**Maja Madirazza:**
然后我添加了一个预览功能。现在，当用户点击预览时，笔记会展开，允许。

**Maja Madirazza:** Allowing them to read it fully before linking it. As
you can see, Figma Make helped me ideate quickly, think visually, and
iterate on the fly.

**Maja Madirazza:** 让他们在链接之前完整地阅读它。正如你所看到的，Figma
Make帮助我快速构思，进行视觉化思考，并即时迭代。

**Maja Madirazza:** Turning one idea into three different variations, I
could share with the product team.

**Maja Madirazza:** 将一个想法变成三个不同的变体，我可以与产品团队分享。

**Maja Madirazza:** With that, I'll pass it over to Christika.

**Maja Madirazza:** 就此，我把话筒交给Christika。

**Krisika Suthan:** Okay, so now I'll talk about our next design pal, AI
as an interaction slash prototyping partner. Here is a mock-up. It's
helpful for aligning with product, engineers, and even users, but one
screen doesn't show the full experience. It's hard to grasp
functionality and flow from a static image. Normally, this is where we
designers prototype, but often we don't always have the time.

**Krisika Suthan:**
好的，现在我来谈谈我们的下一个设计伙伴，AI作为交互/原型设计伙伴。这是一个模型。它有助于与产品、工程师甚至用户对齐，但一个屏幕无法展示完整的体验。从静态图像中很难把握功能和流程。通常，这是我们设计师制作原型的地方，但我们往往没有时间。

**Krisika Suthan:** Or clinical context to build something that is
realistic. Here is where we use Figma Make.

**Krisika Suthan:**
或者没有临床背景来构建一些现实的东西。这就是我们使用Figma Make的地方。

**Krisika Suthan:** So using Figma Make, I turned this mock-up into a
working prototype in just over a half hour. It does not match our
evergreen design system or core, and that is okay.

**Krisika Suthan:** 所以使用Figma
Make，我在半个多小时内就把这个模型变成了一个可工作的原型。它与我们的常青设计系统或核心不匹配，但这没关系。

**Krisika Suthan:** What it does do is bring the mock-up to life,
helping us visualize interaction, workflow, and realistic content
scenarios.

**Krisika Suthan:**
它所做的是让模型活起来，帮助我们可视化交互、工作流程和现实的内容场景。

**Krisika Suthan:** In our recent exploration, we used this to quickly
align with product managers on key ideas. But looking ahead, there is
potential to use these prototypes for user testing and end-to-end.

**Krisika Suthan:**
在我们最近的探索中，我们用它来快速与产品经理就关键想法达成一致。但展望未来，这些原型有潜力用于用户测试和端到端的。

**Krisika Suthan:** Evaluation of feasibility. Passing it down to
Jennifer.

**Krisika Suthan:** 可行性评估。现在交给Jennifer。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Thanks, Krisika. Discoverly is an insight
translator. It's an AI agent I've customized in Copilot to help me share
research findings in real time. I'll show you how it works.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
谢谢，Krisika。Discoverly是一个洞察翻译器。这是我在Copilot中定制的一个AI智能体，用来帮助我实时分享研究发现。我来展示一下它是如何工作的。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Um, before Discoverly, we talked to
customers, highlighted transcripts, summarized key points, created
themes and insights, and then presented the findings.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
在Discoverly之前，我们与客户交谈，高亮转录稿，总结要点，创建主题和洞察，然后展示发现。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Now, we're still talking to customers and
highlighting transcripts, that part's not going to change.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
现在，我们仍然在与客户交谈并高亮转录稿，那部分不会改变。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Um, think of it like data labeling.
Basically, it's helping the AI interpret that data accurately.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
把它想象成数据标注。基本上，它是在帮助AI准确地解释那些数据。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** But now, I can partner with AI to
generate those summaries, themes, and insights in a fraction of the
time, and instantly share them cross-functionally for real-time
collaboration.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
但现在，我可以与AI合作，在极短的时间内生成那些摘要、主题和洞察，并立即跨职能地分享它们，以进行实时协作。

**Jennifer Magana - Product:** Now we can make better decisions
together. Now on to Charlie.

**Jennifer Magana - 产品部:**
现在我们可以一起做出更好的决定。现在交给Charlie。

**Charley Yang:** Thanks, Jen. Now, talking about impact, with tools
like Figma Make and our Custom Research Copilot Agent Discoverly.

**Charley Yang:** 谢谢，Jen。现在，谈到影响，有了像Figma
Make和我们的定制研究Copilot智能体Discoverly这样的工具。

**Charley Yang:** We're accelerating discovery and iteration through
rapid prototyping, quicker synthesis of research insights.

**Charley Yang:**
我们正在通过快速原型制作、更快地综合研究洞察来加速发现和迭代。

**Charley Yang:** And streamlining collaboration to free up time for
more strategic, high-impact design and research.

**Charley Yang:**
并简化协作，以腾出时间进行更具战略性、高影响力的设计和研究。

**Charley Yang:** Moving on into our next slide. So, responsible use of
AI. So, AI tools support our ideas by informing our decisions and
helping us do more at a faster and smarter rate.

**Charley Yang:**
进入下一张幻灯片。所以，负责任地使用AI。AI工具通过为我们的决策提供信息，并帮助我们以更快、更智能的速度做更多的事情来支持我们的想法。

**Charley Yang:** But this is not a substitute for expertise, and it
shouldn't replace human insight in decision making.

**Charley Yang:** 但这不能替代专业知识，也不应取代人类在决策中的洞察力。

**Charley Yang:** When it comes down to our lessons learned,
experimentation is how we learn what works and what doesn't, especially
with AI tools.

**Charley Yang:**
谈到我们的经验教训，实验是我们学习什么有效、什么无效的方式，尤其是在使用AI工具时。

**Charley Yang:** Constant iteration allows us to determine how to move
forward, what to scrap, especially as we are vetting these tools within
our workflows.

**Charley Yang:**
持续的迭代让我们能够决定如何前进，放弃什么，特别是在我们在工作流程中审查这些工具时。

**Charley Yang:** Seguing into our next bullet, as AI evolves, so do we.
We maintain a constant state of learning and adapting our skills as the
tools advance.

**Charley Yang:**
转到下一个要点，随着AI的发展，我们也在发展。我们保持着持续学习的状态，并随着工具的进步调整我们的技能。

**Charley Yang:** Finally, how can it help others? There's no
one-size-fits-all. Every individual and team can shape their own version
of a design pal to fit their needs. If it doesn't work, continue to
iterate, otherwise there's always another tool out there.

**Charley Yang:**
最后，它如何能帮助他人？没有一刀切的解决方案。每个个人和团队都可以塑造自己版本的设计伙伴来满足他们的需求。如果不行，就继续迭代，否则总有其他工具可用。

**Charley Yang:** So, that concludes our presentation. Thank you all for
attending. We'll go ahead and open up the floor to any questions.

**Charley Yang:**
那么，我们的演讲到此结束。谢谢大家的参与。我们现在开放提问环节。

**Marina Stojanovic:** Thank you all, what a wonderful presentation. And
we only have, you know, high fives in the chat for you, so if any
questions do come in later, we'll be sure to share with them with you.

**Marina Stojanovic:**
谢谢大家，多么精彩的演讲。我们在聊天中只有对你们的击掌鼓励，所以如果稍后有任何问题，我们一定会与你们分享。

**Marina Stojanovic:** 交给你了，Kat Canarusa。

### 主持人互动：AI生成图像

chat, uh, we want you to tell us what prompt do you think we use to
generate the image?

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
那么，这是我们下一个“在你等待的时候”。在聊天中，我们希望你告诉我们，你认为我们用什么提示来生成这张图片？

you to figure out what you think we did.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
屏幕上是一个拿着笔记本电脑的人。告诉我们你认为它是什么，在我们等待你弄清楚我们做了什么的时候。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Keki, I want to hear from you. Um…. How has
your experience been using Copilot to generate images?

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
Keki，我想听听你的看法。你使用Copilot生成图像的体验如何？

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Images probably have been the most…. Difficult part

**Ketki Yennemadi:**
图像可能是使用Copilot最……困难的部分，因为它需要大量的迭代。

**Ketki Yennemadi:**
我……当然，它已经变得更好了，但我们仍然会得到那些有11根手指和3只手的图片。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** You know, the typical… so, yes, you know, it
sometimes requires quite a few iterations, but I've also noticed it
doesn't do a very good job with letters. For example.

**Ketki Yennemadi:**
你知道，典型的……所以，是的，你知道，它有时需要相当多的迭代，但我也注意到它在处理字母方面做得不是很好。例如。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** When we were trying to generate a banner for the AI
Symposium, it would give us good images.

**Ketki Yennemadi:**
当我们试图为AI研讨会生成一个横幅时，它会给我们好的图片。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** But not images with AI Symposium written on it. Um,
so yeah, because this is pixel-related, it doesn't do a great job of
identifying.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 但不是带有“AI
Symposium”字样的图片。所以是的，因为这与像素有关，它在识别方面做得不是很好。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 字母和单词。你呢，Arisa？

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** But not with any words, and then I'll use,

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Yeah.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 是的。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 这样它就不会创造出所有奇怪的字母和拼写错误等。

the location you want it to be in.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
我认为你也可以添加很多细节来让这个更具体，对吧？你可以问，比如，你可以添加你希望它在的位置。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Ethnicity, age, type of clothing, specificity,
type of image. All of those details are going to help you get an image
that's closer to what you're looking for.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
种族、年龄、服装类型、具体性、图像类型。所有这些细节都将帮助你得到一张更接近你想要的图片。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** The fleas generate an image of a business

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 但你知道，这可能是基于它训练的一些数据。

**Dave Chodos:** Uh, so yeah, first I wanted to tell you a little bit

**Dave Chodos:**

**Dave Chodos:** 而且……基本上我们试图帮助公司理解的是。

**Dave Chodos:** Are we spending efficiently in the cloud? So, is…. All
this money that we're pouring into the cloud, driving value for
business. Little image here has.

**Dave Chodos:**
我们在云上的花费是否高效？所以，我们投入到云中的所有这些钱，是否在为业务创造价值。这里的小图片有。

**Dave Chodos:** Dollars raining out of the cloud. Really, I want to….
Imagine those dollars kind of getting sucked up into the cloud. It's
kind of the direction that things tend to go.

我们所做任何事情的关键考虑。在这种情况下，我一直在谈论我们如何使用Prophet。我们得到了这些预测，它们准确、有帮助、非常棒。

**Dave Chodos:** But I do want to emphasize that they are not set in
stone.

**Dave Chodos:** 但我确实想强调，它们并非一成不变。

**Dave Chodos:** We don't just take these forecasts and. Charge ahead

us.

**Dave Chodos:**
我们不只是拿了这些预测就盲目地向前冲，说，这就是这个东西的成本。AI告诉我们的。

**Dave Chodos:** We're done. We…. Present those forecasts to the budget

**Dave Chodos:**

**Dave Chodos:** So, for example, if a particular owner knows that their
product is.

**Dave Chodos:** 所以，例如，如果一个特定的负责人知道他们的产品是。

**Dave Chodos:** In, uh, early availability right now, very little
usage. But it's gonna move to limited availability in Q4 and see a jump

**Dave Chodos:**
现在处于早期可用阶段，使用量很少。但它将在第四季度转为有限可用，并出现一个跳跃。

**Dave Chodos:** Mid-september, then…. Lee can indicate in the forecast

**Dave Chodos:**

**Dave Chodos:** That profit, or, you know. Any AI tool like that

**Dave Chodos:**

**Dave Chodos:**

**Dave Chodos:** The AI results don't just wipe it out the next time we

**Dave Chodos:** AI的结果不会在我们下次生成时就把它抹掉。

**Dave Chodos:**

### 用例15：Pawandeep Kaur & Victor Tarnovski - GitHub Copilot在工程中的应用

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Yeah, so for our next use case, we have
Pamdeep. Poindeep and Victor from Engineering on GitHub Copilot. Over to
the two of you!

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
是的，所以我们的下一个用例，我们有Pamdeep。来自工程部的Poindeep和Victor将介绍GitHub
Copilot。交给你们两位了！

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Good afternoon, everyone. Thanks for joining us. My
name is Pavandeep, and I'm here with Victor from Engineering Department
under Tom Andraca.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
大家下午好。感谢你们的加入。我叫Pavandeep，我和来自Tom
Andraca领导的工程部的Victor一起。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Can you see my screen?

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 你能看到我的屏幕吗？

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** We can

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 我们可以。

**Ketki Yennemadi:** Yes, we can.

**Ketki Yennemadi:** 是的，我们可以。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Sorry, let me share it again. Today, we'd like to
share what our team has been working on, and some of the lessons we
learned along the way.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
抱歉，我再分享一次。今天，我们想分享我们团队一直在做的工作，以及我们在此过程中学到的一些教训。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** In March 2023, PointClicker acquired the patient
pattern as a strategic investment to advance value-based care and
better.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 2023年3月，PointClicker收购了Patient
Pattern，作为一项战略投资，以推进基于价值的护理并更好地。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Drive better patient outcomes. Following the early
exists launch in April 2024, stewardship of the product transitioned to
our engineering team.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
推动更好的患者结果。在2024年4月早期版本发布后，产品的管理权移交给了我们的工程团队。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Who brought strong expertise in Java and related
technologies. It became clear that while the product offered substantial
potential, it also presented several unforeseen challenges that require
careful attention moving forward.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
他们在Java和相关技术方面拥有强大的专业知识。很明显，虽然该产品提供了巨大的潜力，但它也带来了一些意想不到的挑战，需要我们在前进中仔细关注。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** From the outset, we recognized there were
significant challenges hidden beneath the surface.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 从一开始，我们就认识到表面之下隐藏着重大的挑战。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** The system had become complex over time. With quick
fixes, workarounds, and evolution from PCC standards, making
improvements slow and unpredictable.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
随着时间的推移，系统变得复杂。由于快速修复、变通方案以及与PCC标准的演变，使得改进变得缓慢且不可预测。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** The front end, inspired by patient pattern theme,
lacked PCC co-design styles.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 前端，受Patient
Pattern主题启发，缺乏PCC的协同设计风格。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Resulting in an inconsistent user experience. While
learning a new language like Python and Django wasn't a challenge,
adapting to the way frameworks were implemented created any extra
hurdles for us.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
导致用户体验不一致。虽然学习像Python和Django这样的新语言不是挑战，但适应框架的实现方式给我们带来了额外的障碍。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Routine changes started to require significant
efforts, and often impacted our performance, reliability, and
scalability.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
常规的变更开始需要巨大的努力，并经常影响我们的性能、可靠性和可扩展性。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Making it clear that we needed a more scalable,
unified foundation to deliver improvements faster and more confidently.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
这清楚地表明，我们需要一个更具可扩展性、更统一的基础，以便更快、更自信地交付改进。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** That's when we decided to try something different,
and bring AI into our transformation journey.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
那时我们决定尝试一些不同的东西，并将AI引入我们的转型之旅。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** We just two engineers, we rebuilt the platform in
three focus phases, all powered by AI.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
我们只有两名工程师，我们在三个重点阶段重建了平台，全部由AI驱动。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** First, we used GitHub Copilot and CloudSonnen to
untangle the maze.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 首先，我们使用GitHub
Copilot和CloudSonnen来解开这个迷宫。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Mapping workflows, doing class-by-class comparisons,
and building testament blueprints. This let everyone, engineers and
business folks, get streamlined.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
映射工作流程，进行逐类比较，并构建测试蓝图。这让每个人，无论是工程师还是业务人员，都能简化流程。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Next, put up those blueprints and put AI to work.
Migrating key modules.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 接下来，拿出那些蓝图，让AI开始工作。迁移关键模块。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** From Python to Java, modernizing the front end with
React, and connecting it all with mermaid diagrams, so we could catch
issues early.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
从Python到Java，用React现代化前端，并用Mermaid图（一种用于生成图表和流程图的标记语言）将所有东西连接起来，这样我们就能及早发现问题。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** In just one week, we had a working prototype.
Finally, we polish the product.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
仅仅一周，我们就有了可工作的原型。最后，我们打磨产品。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Iterating plot, performance gains, and catching
security vulnerabilities. Beyond the speed, what stood out most was the
clarity and assurance AI brought to our design.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
迭代情节、性能提升和捕捉安全漏洞。除了速度，最突出的是AI为我们的设计带来的清晰度和保证。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** And making decisions. And how it was making our
decisions.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 并做出决定。以及它如何做出我们的决定。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Very impactful. So what's… what did this
transformation mean for our team and our users?

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
非常有影响力。那么……这次转型对我们的团队和用户意味着什么？

**Pawandeep Kaur:** First, this transformation could reduce development
effort from one's estimated at 400 engineering hours.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
首先，这次转型可以将开发工作量从估计的400个工程小时减少。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** To just 20, allowing us to deliver value to
customers weeks sooner.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 到仅仅20小时，让我们能提前数周向客户交付价值。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** With improvement testing and streamlined workflows,
we can lower support. Needs and could strengthen user trust.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
通过改进测试和简化的工作流程，我们可以降低支持需求，并能增强用户信任。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Our system could handle twice the workload on the
same hardware without degrading the expected latency.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
我们的系统可以在相同的硬件上处理两倍的工作负载，而不会降低预期的延迟。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** We were able to automate 30% of repetitive tasks,
which was one of our greatest wins.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
我们能够自动化30%的重复性任务，这是我们最大的胜利之一。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** These benefits are based on measurable gains we saw
in our pilot version, demonstrating what's possible as we scale these
improvements.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
这些好处是基于我们在试点版本中看到的可衡量收益，展示了当我们扩展这些改进时可能实现的目标。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Looking back…. Uh, a few lessons really stand out.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 回顾过去……有几个教训非常突出。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** First, mapping out our workflows made a huge
difference. It turned uncertainty into clarity.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
首先，规划我们的工作流程带来了巨大的变化。它将不确定性变成了清晰。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Second, AI is a powerful tool. For speed and scale,
but it's the expertise of our people that ensures quality.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
其次，AI是一个强大的工具。在速度和规模方面，但确保质量的是我们员工的专业知识。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** And finally, quick wins matter. Every small success
builds momentum and helps teams stay engaged.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
最后，快速的胜利很重要。每一个小成功都会建立势头，并帮助团队保持参与。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** This approach isn't unique to our journey. Any PCC
team can take these steps, make work visible, combine AI with human
judgment.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
这种方法并非我们旅程独有。任何PCC团队都可以采取这些步骤，让工作可见，将AI与人类判断相结合。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** And keep moving forward. With this, I'll hand it
over to my colleague, who will walk us through a live demo.

**Pawandeep Kaur:**
并继续前进。就此，我把话筒交给我的同事，他将带我们进行现场演示。

**Pawandeep Kaur:** Of what this transformation looks like in action.

**Pawandeep Kaur:** 关于这次转型在实际行动中的样子。
