### 用例16：Erik Stabile & Arush Sharma - 安全计划助手

**Erik Stabile:** Great. Um, thank you so much, everybody. Sorry for the
delay there. Um, I'm just gonna share my….

**Erik Stabile:** 太好了。非常感谢大家。抱歉耽搁了。我这就分享我的……

**Erik Stabile:** Screen here….

**Erik Stabile:** 屏幕在这里……

**Erik Stabile:** Okay, everything look good? You should be able to see
my screen.

**Erik Stabile:** 好的，一切看起来都好吗？你应该能看到我的屏幕。

**Erik Stabile:** Um, my name is Eric Stabil, I'm Product Marketing
Manager, and today I'll be presenting on the security.

**Erik Stabile:** 我叫Eric
Stabil，是产品市场经理，今天我将就安全问题进行演讲。

**Erik Stabile:** Program assistant on behalf of myself and Arush
Sharma, Senior Product Manager.

**Erik Stabile:** 我代表我自己和高级产品经理Arush
Sharma，介绍这个项目助手。

**Erik Stabile:** Uh, together in part with Rafat, uh, Rajudin, we used
Copilot Studios to tackle a challenge that we faced during the rollout
of our new security enhancements.

**Erik Stabile:** 我们与Rafat Rajudin部分合作，使用Copilot
Studios来解决我们在推出新的安全增强功能时面临的一个挑战。

**Erik Stabile:** Uh, for point-click care customers.

**Erik Stabile:** 为PointClickCare的客户。

**Erik Stabile:** Uh, when we launched our latest round of security
enhancements, we were flooded with questions from internal support
teams.

**Erik Stabile:**
当我们推出最新一轮的安全增强功能时，我们收到了来自内部支持团队的大量问题。

**Erik Stabile:** Customer success managers and customers. But the
answers…. Were often complex and specific. They were scattered across
multiple resources, making it difficult for teams to find consistent,
timely information, slowing down response times and increasing support
overhead.

**Erik Stabile:**
客户成功经理和客户。但答案……通常复杂且具体。它们分散在多个资源中，使得团队难以找到一致、及时的信息，从而减慢了响应时间并增加了支持开销。

**Erik Stabile:** To solve this problem, we introduced an AI-powered
agent embedded directly in Microsoft Teams and trained on all of our
relevant customer-facing content.

**Erik Stabile:** 为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一个直接嵌入到Microsoft
Teams中的AI驱动的智能体，并用我们所有相关的面向客户的内容对其进行了训练。

**Erik Stabile:** Now, instead of digging through lengthy FAQs, guides,
and slide decks, team members could simply ask the AI.

**Erik Stabile:**
现在，团队成员不必再翻阅冗长的常见问题解答、指南和幻灯片，他们可以直接问AI。

**Erik Stabile:** And receive context-aware responses. This reduced
response times, improving consistency, and freeing staff to focus on
higher-value work.

**Erik Stabile:**
并收到具有上下文感知的回应。这减少了响应时间，提高了信息的一致性，并让员工能专注于更高价值的工作。

**Erik Stabile:** Um, since launch, the agent has powered 150-plus
sessions with a 75% engagement rate.

**Erik Stabile:**
自推出以来，该智能体已支持超过150次会话，参与率达到75%。

**Erik Stabile:** And a 4 out of 5 satisfaction score among internal
users.

**Erik Stabile:** 在内部用户中获得了5分制中的4分满意度。

**Erik Stabile:** Uh, during live office hours, so we host weekly office
hours every week to answer customer questions around MFA.

**Erik Stabile:**
在现场办公时间，我们每周都会举办办公时间，回答客户关于MFA（多因素认证）的问题。

**Erik Stabile:** Um, during live office hours, it's empowered a
panelist to answer roughly one question per minute in real time.

**Erik Stabile:**
在现场办公时间，它赋能了一位小组成员，使其能实时地大约每分钟回答一个问题。

**Erik Stabile:** Boosting productivity and reducing friction for
customers. And of course, to be responsible, we added a disclaimer
reminding users to verify AI-generated content.

**Erik Stabile:**
提高了生产力，并减少了客户的摩擦。当然，为了负责任，我们添加了一个免责声明，提醒用户验证AI生成的内容。

**Erik Stabile:** For accuracy, uh, keeping our standards high while
moving fast. Um, so with that, I'm going to pass this off to Arush for
our demo.

**Erik Stabile:**
为了准确性，在快速行动的同时保持我们的高标准。那么，就此，我将把话筒交给Arush进行我们的演示。

**Erik Stabile:** Let's see here…. Let's take a behind-the-scenes look
at how you can create an agent for your use case.

**Erik Stabile:**
让我们看看……让我们来看看幕后，看看你如何为你的用例创建一个智能体。

**Erik Stabile:** At the top of the screen, you'll find the section
where you can enter a description.

**Erik Stabile:** 在屏幕顶部，你会找到一个可以输入描述的部分。

**Erik Stabile:** And define the purpose or objective of your agent.
Next, define the instructions for the security program assistant.

**Erik Stabile:**
并定义你的智能体的目的或目标。接下来，定义安全程序助手的指令。

**Erik Stabile:** Remember, the more specific your instructions are, the
more accurate the agent's responses will be.

**Erik Stabile:** 记住，你的指令越具体，智能体的回应就越准确。

**Erik Stabile:** You can turn on generative orchestration. This enables
the agent to use generative AI.

**Erik Stabile:** 你可以开启生成式编排。这使智能体能够使用生成式AI。

**Erik Stabile:** To decide how it responds. Making conversations more
natural and fluid for the user.

**Erik Stabile:** 来决定如何回应。让用户的对话更自然、更流畅。

**Erik Stabile:** Within Copilot Studio, knowledge sources work
alongside generative answers. When you add a knowledge source, your
agent can tap into enterprise data, whether it's from internal systems.

**Erik Stabile:** 在Copilot
Studio中，知识源与生成式答案协同工作。当你添加一个知识源时，你的智能体可以利用企业数据，无论它来自内部系统。

**Erik Stabile:** Public websites or external platforms. You can simply
drag and drop a file, or choose from the data sources listed below.

**Erik Stabile:**
公共网站或外部平台。你可以简单地拖放一个文件，或者从下面列出的数据源中选择。

**Erik Stabile:** In this setup, we've added SharePoint, along with
customer-facing. Documentation and help files.

**Erik Stabile:**
在这个设置中，我们添加了SharePoint，以及面向客户的文档和帮助文件。

**Erik Stabile:** And just recently, they released a new feature that
lets you integrate MCP servers too.

**Erik Stabile:**
最近，他们发布了一个新功能，让你也可以集成MCP（微软认证专家）服务器。

**Erik Stabile:** Rules in a co-pilot agent allow your agent to take
action beyond just answering questions.

**Erik Stabile:**
Copilot智能体中的规则允许你的智能体采取超越仅仅回答问题的行动。

**Erik Stabile:** They can trigger workflows, call APIs. Query
databases, or even perform tasks like resetting passwords or updating
records.

**Erik Stabile:**
它们可以触发工作流程，调用API，查询数据库，甚至执行像重置密码或更新记录这样的任务。

**Erik Stabile:** All based on user input. Think of tools as the hands
of your agent.

**Erik Stabile:** 全部基于用户输入。把工具想象成你智能体的手。

**Erik Stabile:** While the generative AI is the brain. Together, they
make the agent not just conversational, but truly functional.

**Erik Stabile:**
而生成式AI是大脑。它们共同使智能体不仅能对话，而且真正具有功能性。

**Erik Stabile:** Agents can work together by connecting with other
agents. This means your primary agent can delegate specific parts of a
workflow to another agent that's dedicated to handling those steps.

**Erik Stabile:**
智能体可以通过与其他智能体连接来协同工作。这意味着你的主智能体可以将工作流程的特定部分委托给另一个专门处理这些步骤的智能体。

**Erik Stabile:** It's a powerful way to break down complex processes.
Keep things modular, and ensure each agent focuses on what it does best.

**Erik Stabile:**
这是分解复杂流程的强大方式。保持模块化，并确保每个智能体都专注于它最擅长的事情。

**Erik Stabile:** While still delivering a seamless experience to the
user.

**Erik Stabile:** 同时仍然为用户提供无缝的体验。

**Erik Stabile:** Once your agent is ready, you can publish it directly
to Microsoft Teams.

**Erik Stabile:** 一旦你的智能体准备好了，你可以直接将它发布到Microsoft
Teams。

**Erik Stabile:** This makes the agent easily accessible to users within
your organization, right where they already collaborate.

**Erik Stabile:**
这使得你组织内的用户可以轻松访问这个智能体，就在他们已经协作的地方。

**Erik Stabile:** And communicate. It appears just like a regular Teams
app. It's a fast way to bring automation and support directly into daily
work conversations.

**Erik Stabile:**
并进行沟通。它看起来就像一个普通的Teams应用。这是一种将自动化和支持直接带入日常工作对话的快速方式。

**Erik Stabile:** This agent isn't just about saving time. It's about
reclaiming our attention for the work that matters most.

**Erik Stabile:**
这个智能体不仅仅是为了节省时间。它是为了让我们重新关注最重要的工作。

**Erik Stabile:** The problems that don't have obvious answers. If
you've ever thought someone should automate this.

**Erik Stabile:**
那些没有明显答案的问题。如果你曾想过有人应该自动化这个。

**Erik Stabile:** Searching, or there's got to be a smarter way. Then
take this as your sign.

**Erik Stabile:** 搜索，或者一定有更聪明的方法。那么就把这当作你的信号。

**Erik Stabile:** You're the someone. Built the agent you wish you had.
All right, thank you. Uh, any questions?

**Erik Stabile:**
你就是那个人。构建你希望拥有的智能体。好的，谢谢你。有什么问题吗？

**Erik Stabile:** And I'm happy to take those offline as well.

**Erik Stabile:** 我也很乐意在线下回答这些问题。

**Marina Stojanovic:** I do see, um, one question in the…. Chat, sorry,
in the Q&A. Is this live, or is it in POC?

**Marina Stojanovic:**
我确实在……聊天，抱歉，在问答区看到了一个问题。这是已经上线了，还是在概念验证（POC）阶段？

**Erik Stabile:** This is live. Yep, it's being used right now. We've
been using this for….

**Erik Stabile:** 这已经上线了。是的，现在正在使用。我们已经使用这个……

**Erik Stabile:** Almost, I would say, about a month now, um, and we
actively use it on a weekly basis, uh, especially during our.

**Erik Stabile:**
我想说，差不多一个月了，我们每周都会积极使用它，特别是在我们的。

**Erik Stabile:** Um, weekly customer Q&A sessions.

**Erik Stabile:** 每周客户问答环节。

### 主持人互动：AI预测未来职业

you could just share the screen for us, that would be awesome.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**

to be using.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 我会把我们将要使用的提示放进去。

**Lisa Jarrett:**

**Lisa Jarrett:** 所以……我们的客户指望我们，对吧，为他们做负责任的事情。

**Lisa Jarrett:** 他们不一定有资源去……去深入审视所有这些不同的维度。

**Lisa Jarrett:** 所以当我们推进我们产品的AI部分时。

**Lisa Jarrett:**

**Lisa Jarrett:** 对正在使用的数据源保持透明。所以有很多不同的维度。

**Lisa Jarrett:** 我要说的最后一点是，这不是一次性的事情。

**Lisa Jarrett:** 当你把一个AI能力放到一个产品里时。

**Lisa Jarrett:**

**Dean Slawson:** Well, and this is something we partner closely with,

**Dean Slawson:**

**Dean Slawson:**

**Dean Slawson:** And so, this is something we proactively look at
during the AI model development process.

**Dean Slawson:** 所以，这是我们在AI模型开发过程中主动关注的事情。

**Dean Slawson:** Um, we do, you know, binary classification, we see if.
If different groups are differentially giving different outputs to a
model, so it's something that we measure, it's something that we
evaluate.

**Dean Slawson:**
我们做，你知道，二元分类，我们看是否。如果不同的群体对一个模型给出不同的输出，所以这是我们衡量的事情，是我们评估的事情。

**Dean Slawson:** Um, and things Lisa was talking about, something we
continue to measure even after we deploy, because there could be shifts
in population or data or biases that get introduced later.

**Dean Slawson:**
而且Lisa谈到的事情，是我们即使在部署后也会继续衡量的事情，因为可能会有人口或数据的变化，或者后来引入的偏见。

**Dean Slawson:** But it's also something that we work to mitigate, you
know, and sometimes.

**Dean Slawson:** 但这也是我们努力减轻的事情，你知道，有时。

**Dean Slawson:** You can change the threshold of a model and address,
you know, most of the bias issues, or sometimes.

**Dean Slawson:**
你可以改变一个模型的阈值，并解决，你知道，大部分的偏见问题，或者有时。

**Dean Slawson:** Um, a lot of it is communicating properly, you know,
so that users understand what, you know, things they need to be aware
of, because you can't 100% eliminate bias.

**Dean Slawson:**
很多时候是正确地沟通，你知道，这样用户就能理解他们需要注意什么，因为你不能100%消除偏见。

**Dean Slawson:** We obviously don't want to ship something. That's
going to be harmful to any group, but we also want to create, sort of,
the greater good, and.

**Dean Slawson:**
我们显然不想发布任何会对任何群体有害的东西，但我们也想创造，某种程度上，更大的利益，并且。

**Dean Slawson:** Um, it's, uh, it's always a focus of attention and a
balance to make sure that what we ship is responsible, and that users
understand any limitations of it.

**Dean Slawson:**
这始终是一个关注的焦点和一个平衡，以确保我们发布的产品是负责任的，并且用户理解它的任何局限性。

**Jared Pilcher:** 双脚跳进去，学习你能学到的一切。关于……

**Jared Pilcher:** Llms, about agents. Um, and uh… and then try to push
the envelope.

**Jared Pilcher:**
LLM（大型语言模型），关于智能体。然后……然后试着挑战极限。

**Jared Pilcher:** Um, sooner. That's what I would tell myself.

**Jared Pilcher:** 更早。这就是我会告诉自己的。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** There actually is an agent on Copilot that's
called Learning Coach, which can help you develop, like, a learning plan
to learn. So you can use AI to learn about AI as well.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
Copilot上实际上有一个叫做“学习教练”的智能体，它可以帮助你制定一个学习计划。所以你也可以用AI来学习AI。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Um, because I think the hardest thing is
finding time, and you know, what do you learn, and what do you focus on,
and so it can actually ask you certain questions to figure out what
might make most sense for you to get deeper knowledge on.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
因为我认为最难的是找到时间，而且你知道，你学什么，你专注于什么，所以它实际上可以问你一些问题，来弄清楚什么对你来说最有意义，以获得更深入的知识。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** So with that, I'm going to thank all of our
panelists. Thank you so much for sharing your insights and opinions
about what's coming up for us in AI and how it's going to affect the
healthcare space.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
就此，我要感谢我们所有的小组成员。非常感谢你们分享你们对AI未来发展以及它将如何影响医疗健康领域的见解和看法。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Uh, we can give them a virtual… well, you can
hear me, so I will cough. Uh, but we'll give you a virtual round of
applause. Thank you for sharing your thoughts.

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:**
我们可以给他们一个虚拟的……嗯，你能听到我，所以我咳嗽一下。但我们会给你一个虚拟的掌声。谢谢你分享你的想法。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** And I'm seeing some of the pause coming in the

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** 我也看到聊天中出现了一些暂停。

**Auroosa Kazmi-Ishaq:** Uh, now we will transition over to our closing,

## 闭幕致辞：回顾与展望

**Dr. Cindy Plunkett:**

**Dr. Cindy Plunkett:**

**Dr. Cindy Plunkett:** 始终是必需的。始终仔细检查AI生成的响应至关重要。

**Dr. Cindy Plunkett:**
